        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

I could not repro the issue. The problem is that the entry in `throughput_tracker_map_` is removed when `StopThroughtputTracker` is called. Currently, this is protected by a DCHECK and I could not get it to happen and I could not repro with an asan build either.

Fix tab hover card overlapping animation edge case



<span class="line"><!---->Fix tab hover card overlapping animation edge case<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





There is one edge case that "TabHoverCardController::HideHoverCard



<span class="line"><!---->There is one edge case that "TabHoverCardController::HideHoverCard<!----></span>



<br>





-> WidgetFadeAnimator::FadeOut" could be called with an active



<span class="line"><!---->-&gt; WidgetFadeAnimator::FadeOut" could be called with an active<!----></span>



<br>





fade in animation. WidgetFadeAnimator::Hide would directly close



<span class="line"><!---->fade in animation. WidgetFadeAnimator::Hide would directly close<!----></span>



<br>





the card widget in such case. However, there is an active



<span class="line"><!---->the card widget in such case. However, there is an active<!----></span>



<br>





ui::ThroughputTracker because of the unfinished fade-in animation.



<span class="line"><!---->ui::ThroughputTracker because of the unfinished fade-in animation.<!----></span>



<br>





Stop() would be triggered twice in WidgetFadeAnimator::FadeOut



<span class="line"><!---->Stop() would be triggered twice in WidgetFadeAnimator::FadeOut<!----></span>



<br>





for the edge case. Once from `fade_complete_callbacks_.Notify`



<span class="line"><!---->for the edge case. Once from `fade_complete_callbacks_.Notify`<!----></span>



<br>





and the other one from WidgetFadeAnimator::OnWidgetDestroying. The



<span class="line"><!---->and the other one from WidgetFadeAnimator::OnWidgetDestroying. The<!----></span>



<br>





2nd Stop() would cause a crash because the tracker is no longer



<span class="line"><!---->2nd Stop() would cause a crash because the tracker is no longer<!----></span>



<br>





valid in ui::Compositor.



<span class="line"><!---->valid in ui::Compositor.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL fixes the crash by canceling the pending fade-in animation



<span class="line"><!---->This CL fixes the crash by canceling the pending fade-in animation<!----></span>



<br>





and resets the tracker for the edge case.



<span class="line"><!---->and resets the tracker for the edge case.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

I was wrong about the DCHECK in #10. It is actually the cause of double Stop().



<span class="line"><!---->I was wrong about the DCHECK in #10. It is actually the cause of double Stop().<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Check out code around the DCHECK:



<span class="line"><!---->Check out code around the DCHECK:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/views/animation/widget_fade_animator.cc;drc=287fa204b78ccaa8da5c1a155c5fbfacafef31c8;l=42-45



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/views/animation/widget_fade_animator.cc;drc=287fa204b78ccaa8da5c1a155c5fbfacafef31c8;l=42-45"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/views/animation/widget_fade_animator.cc;drc=287fa204b78ccaa8da5c1a155c5fbfacafef31c8;l=42-45<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





When the DCHECK is triggered, FadeOut() is called with a running fade-in animation. The code would trigger Stop() twice. Once from `fade_complete_callbacks_.Notify` and the other from `widget_->Close()` -> `WidgetFadeAnimator::OnWidgetDestroying`. The 2nd Stop is the crash in #0.



<span class="line"><!---->When the DCHECK is triggered, FadeOut() is called with a running fade-in animation. The code would trigger Stop() twice. Once from `fade_complete_callbacks_.Notify` and the other from `widget_-&gt;Close()` -&gt; `WidgetFadeAnimator::OnWidgetDestroying`. The 2nd Stop is the crash in #0.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Think the CL in #20 should fix the issue.



<span class="line"><!---->Think the CL in #20 should fix the issue.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);

          border-collapse: collapse;

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
